1b1(rgyud): // spyan 'dren rgyud gsum pa/ bla ma'i blam bla med dkon mchog gsum/ 
1b2(rgyud): ba'i tshe mchog dbang mchog dam pa la// gus pas phyag 'tshal dang bas skyabs su mchi/ 
1b3(rgyud): gnam sa'i mnga' bdag skye dgu'i longs spyod gzhi// bstan pa dam pa chos kyi mgon mdzad
1b4(rgyud): pa// tshangs pa brgya byin rgyal chen yul 'khor srung // 'phags skyes mig mi bzang dang
1b5(rgyud): lus ngan po// 'jig rten skyong ba dbang po mi lha dang // gshin rje bdeni bral chulha rlung gi lha// 
2a1(rgyud): // rnam thos bu dang dbang bdag sa yi lha// nyi zla gza' skar phyogs kyi glang po rnams// blon po sde dpon lha mo phyogs
2a2(rgyud): mtshams srung // btsun skyem bcas su so la khyer gan ba// sku sa sted pon chen por mtshan grags ge// khye 'jug
2a3(rgyud): tshogs bdag nan ti kar ti ka/ nag po chen po stobs chen stobs po che// gnod 'dzin pa dam pad ma chen po dang // dung
2a4(rgyud): dung chen gang po shin du gang // mgrin bzang gang ba bzang po nor 'u bzang // bum rna dril na rna gsum rna po che// gang dag gi
2a5(rgyud): dang yang dag rgyal ba dang // rgyal ba'i khyu mchog 'phrog gnas gangs la gnas// bder lngas rtsen lnga len tshigs lnga
2a6(rgyud): mgrin bcu rnam 'jigs 'brug sman ma mkha'i dbyangs// stong gsum rgya mtsho dga' bo bsnyen dga' bo// ma dros gzi
2b1(rgyud): can nor rgyas gdon la 'jebs// drang srong rig 'dzin mar sprin lo tog lnga// lam lha nyin mtshan dus mtshams tshes grangs yud// ha nu pan ta la sogs mthu chen dang // tshig dbang lha mo
2b2(rgyud): dbyangs dbyangs can dang // be'u 'dra dpal gyi lha mo 'ong zer can// dper sham brjid skyobo gang gis mun// sras rabar dang can ri mkhar nag mo dang // ma bdun phreng mo bdun dang sri mdzin/ 
2b3(rgyud): nag mo chen mo ral pa gcig la sogs// lha mo chen mo gnod sbyin chen mo dang // srin mo chen mo sha za chen ma dang // gzhon nu'i sku 'tsho rdzu 'phrul dbang gis 'phags// smag chen brjid pa lba
2b4(rgyud): yul du bstod// rmang grags chen po'i dge bsnyen chen po dang // lha skyas gzhon nu klu sras gzhon nu dang / ka rid 'dzin gzhon nu drang srong gzhon nu dang // bik+Shus bsten pa'i gzhon nu lnga pa
2b5(rgyud): sman// gnod sbyin grazhon nu ti r+ya ka la sogs// gzi brjid chen po'i gzhon sde thams cid dang // skye dgu'i bdag po la sogs lce dang kA/ gnod sbyin dri zla lce'i bye lha ma yin// gser 'dres
2b6(rgyud): ma srin po mi 'om ci// 'byung po sha za yul bdag 'dre la sogs// cang shes snying rje'i lam du zhugos dgu dang // rig pa'i lcags kyus zin pa kun gson cig/ gang gi ming la'ang bkra shi
2b7(rgyud): dpal 'bar ba// yi ge gnyis 'brel dkon mchog gsum gyi mtshan// skyes bu ga' zhig nyan tam 'don pa yang // gzha' gsang yun gyi chu srid 'thob 'gyur na// yon tan bun kub dpag
2b8(rgyud): yas dkon mchog la// bsnyen bkur ma nyes byed bga' la gus pa dang // chos thos gams su len pa ci zhig smom// de bas gsung rab dpag bsam rgyas pa yi// lha yi longs spyod tshal du phun
3a1(rgyud): gshegs te// chos rje nya ma thams cad mkhyen pa'i bkang // bdud snga lha men g.yul las rgyal byed pa// rin chen 'od mchog lha dbang gtsug gi rgyan// khag yod dad pa'i spyi
3a2(rgyud): bar mdzod// kye rgyal ba'i sras khyod tshur shog/ bdag dang sems can kun kyang yongs su mya ngan las 'das par bgyis la/ sems can ma rgal bas ma 'jigs par bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshe
3a3(rgyud): btsal bas mi ngoms pa la sems zhog cig/ mngon par 'du byed pa'i rang bzhin gyi mtshan nyid kyang ma gtang zhig/ sangs rgyas kyi gzugs kyi sku yang mdor cig/ 'dod chags dang bral ba'ang
3a4(rgyud): par gyis shig/ chos thams cad la chags pa med pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyang btsal bar gyis shig/ chos thams cad la gzhan gyi dring 'jog pa med par sangs rgyas kyi ning yang
3a5(rgyud): su spyad par gyis shig/ zhing gi mtshan nyid nam mkha' lta bur yang shes par gyis shig/ sems can yongs su smin par bya bas ma skyo shig/ bdag med pa'i mtshan nyid kyang ma spongs shig/ ma
3a6(rgyud): ro shes pa la yang rnam par 'phrul bar gyis shig/ chos kyi dbyings las kyang ma g.yo zhig/ byang chub tu sems bskyed pa yang ma gtang zhig/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la yang 'byung
3a7(rgyud): kyis shig/ chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas sems can thams cad tshim par gyis shig/ chos nyid brjod du med pa las kyang 'da' bar ma byed cig/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'brel
3a8(rgyud): na gyi brlabs kyang yongs su ston cig/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus kyang mdor cig/ skye ba'i skye mched thams cad du yang snang bar gyi sa shig yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba chen po yang
3b1(rgyud): susngon cig ces/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di dag ni lta ba'i chos zung dang snrel nur sgrub pa mngon par bslab pa rnams nye bar sgrub pa pa de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi phrin las yang dag phul gyi chos bcu pa zhes bya
3b2(rgyud): kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams rang byung gi phrin las gzhan gyi dring 'jog pa med par bla na med pa'i byang chub 'tho
3b3(rgyud): bar 'gyur ba dag go// lha yi rgyal po dbang chen mchog sbyin gtso// dpa' bo 'jigs med 'jig rten kun la grags// shes rab rod gsal zla ba nya ba'i zhal// skyes mchog smon lam phrin las gcig
3b4(rgyud): pa'i mched// tshangs pa brgya byin 'jig rten slob la sogs// rdo rje ting 'dzin ri rab srub shing dang // snying rje brtson 'grus klu yi sru zag gis// shes rab chen po'i rgya mtsho bsrubs pa'i bcud / 
3b5(rgyud): bdud rtsi'i 'gron du gshegs kun la// chos bsgrags bsod nams dbyig kyang spyir 'bul gyis// srin dmag lha min g.yul las rgyal ba dang // lha yi rgyal srid nga'u mog brtsan par bsngo// ga
3b6(rgyud): g.yog 'khor longs spyod 'phel ba dang // mthu rtsal go 'phang khyad par thob par bso// rdzu 'phrul mngon shes pa rol phyin la sogs/ rnam par thar pa'i blo kun rdzogs pa dang // dge ba'i phrin las dgong sad
3b7(rgyud): grub par bsngo// dam chos bdud rtsi'i bde bas lus khyab ste// sdug bsngal gnod pa'i rgyud las grol bar bsngo// dge ba'i bshes gnyen bka' drin byams pa'i gnyen// bdag cag nyon mongs mchod
3b8(rgyud): rnam rnams/ khrugs rje'i byin kyi brlabs kyis bskya ba dang // gang gis gal sa skye la du byed ci// de bzhin gshegs la le bstan pa bsrung bar gsol// ma 'os 'phrul pa'i nongs pa mchis so
4a1(rgyud): dus rig rgyud mkhyen kun la bzod par gsol// lha tshogs rgyas kyi sbyin par bkra shas gyis// phun sum tshogs 'dzin dam chos rgyas par smon// rgyud gsum pa rdzogs s+ho// chu dgas
4a2(rgyud): / tshangs pa brgya byin rgyal chen lha dang klu/ gnod sbyin dri ba lho phye lha ma yin// gsor 'dab grul bum ma'amache la sogs// sems can gang dag bde gshegs sras rnams dang // nor 'dun phun sa
4a3(rgyud): dpal bzhed kun gson cig/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan yon tan bsam mi khyag// dam pa'i chos kyi yon tan bsam mi khyab// 'phags pa'i dge 'dun yon tan bsam mi khyab// dkon mchog bsam mi khyab la
4a4(rgyud): mngon dad pa'i// rnam smin bla na med pa'ang bsam mi khyab// bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig bgrang bar yang // dkon mchog mtshan thos tsam yang
4a5(rgyud): rdzu 'phrul dad pa'i shugs kyis 'dir gshegs te// rnam par grol ba'i rin chen sna tshogs gling // zab mo rgyal ba'i bka' la kun gson cig/ bsngo ba gang dag dam chos lhur led 'dingar 'dus pa/ 
4a6(rgyud): gdod sbyin la sogs mthu chen rnams// chos kyi bsod rnams shas kyang khyed bzhes te// gzi byin 'khor 'phel dgongs pa 'grub par bsngo// gsung rab bdud brtsi'i rjes su sbubs mdzod la// 
4a7(rgyud): / rigs so sor dpal bskyed cing // de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa bsrung bar gsol// rgyud gsum pa rdzogs s+ho/ 66/ rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya rang no la ka nA ma d+hA ra tI ma hA yA nu sU \u0f7f/ bongs
4a8(rgyud): dra/ 'phags pa dkon mchog tal la'i gzungs shes bya ba theg pa chen po'i ma'o// sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tsham la 'di snyed pa dag gis thos pa dus
4b1(rgyud): gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das rgyal po'i khab na/ bya rgod kyi phung po'i rel dge slong stong du tshang ba thams cad kyang dkar po'i chos yongs su rdzogs pa/ seng ge'i sa chen po sgrog pa/ ye shes kyi tshogs
4b2(rgyud): dpag tu med pa chel byal mkhas pa sha stag gi dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po dang mabs gcig tu bzhugs so// byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun chen po 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems pa
4b3(rgyud): chen po kun du bzang po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag rA phyag rgya rin po che dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rtag tu
4b4(rgyud): chen po yon tan gyis brgyan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bsod namar mngon par bsgrags dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po blo gros chen po dang / byang chub sam
4b5(rgyud): dpa' sems dpa' chen pa yon tan bkod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i blo gros dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa
4b6(rgyud): sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i 'od dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje mtshon cha dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje sra pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa
4b7(rgyud): bos 'dzin dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gzungs kyi blo gros dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po don kun mthong dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sgra
4b8(rgyud): sa gzigs dbang phyug dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mthu chen thob dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po blo gros brtan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
5a1(rgyud): po lag na rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po 'jam dpal gzhan nur gyur pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ngan song stong bar dang bya
5a2(rgyud): dpa' sems dpa' chen po myangangan dang ldan pa thams cad 'joms pa dang / byang chubasams dpa' samos dpa yi yongs kyi rgyal gyis rnam par gad pa dang / byang chubs sa pa sems
5a3(rgyud): sa le mi 'dong ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po can na snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po blo gros rgya mche dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
5a4(rgyud): dka' dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dga' 'byung dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyod pa'i blo gros dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
5a5(rgyud): na po spongs pa brtsegs dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mgyogs pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa dang / de dag la sogs pa kyang
5a6(rgyud): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam par thar pa bsam gyis me khyab pa la gnas pa/ dpa' bar 'gro ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyis nges par 'byung ba/ dbyangs sgra thogs pa med pa/ sangs rgyas kyi nang du
5a7(rgyud): med pa zil gyis gnod pa la mkhas pa/ mi 'jigs pa la gnas pa/ rjes su chags pa dang khong khro ba dang bral ba/ yid du 'ong ba'i dbyangs dang ldan pa/ khams gsum lam chags pa/ g.yog la
5a8(rgyud): mi phyed pa dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid las nges par skyes pa/ ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ re ba thams cad yongs su skong ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
5b1(rgyud): gas par khang du chud pa/ lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las kya mtha'aded yod pa lams pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la mngod par brtson gting nge 'dzid dang spyod pa tshad med par byin gyis brlabs pa ma
5b2(rgyud): pathob pa/ stong pa nyid stong yul ba mtshan ma med pa la gnas pa shasug dang yang thabs cig go/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun du bzang po nas bya ba 'khor de nyid du 'dus par gyur
5b3(rgyud): 'dug pa dus bcom ldan 'das kyi 'bras la mgo pas phyag 'tshal rnas bcom ldan 'das ma 'di skad ces gso to// com ldan 'dus chos ca kya seM myung rtogs par gyi/ bcom ldan 'das kyi
5b4(rgyud): stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu chos kyi dbyings ni dngos po med par rtogs par bya'o// rigs kyi bu chos kyi dbyings ni nam mkha' dang mtshungs pa dang / spros pa med pa dang ma spros pa dang blang ba med pa dang dor ba med pa dang dngos po
5b5(rgyud): dang / gnas pa med pa ste ltar rtogs par bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos gsol pa / bcom ldan 'das ci lags/ chos kyi dbyangs byung ba nam sam/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsa
5b6(rgyud): rigs kyi bu chos kyi dbyings ni 'byung ba med pa'o// rigs kyi bu chos kyi dbyings ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// rigs kyi bu chos kyi dbyings ni dngos po med pa rtogs pa ste/ ro po gang du yang brjod par bya ba ma
5b7(rgyud): nga bstan par byab ma yin pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' kun du zang pas gsol pa/ btsam ldan 'das byang chub la rnam pa du mches/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi pa byang chub kyi rnam
5b8(rgyud): med de de ni tshad dang ldan par bstan par mi nus so// byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos gsol pa/ bcom lda
6a1(rgyud): kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu chos kyi dbyings ni rnam par mi rtog go// byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gapa te chos kyi dbyangs rnam par mi
6a2(rgyud): pa lags na/ byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams ci'i slad du rtog par bgyid/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi babris pa so so'i sa po thams cad ni rtog pa dang / rnam par rtog 'dang / yongs
6a3(rgyud): rtog pa las byung ba'o// byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi byang chubo ni zeb lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal
6a4(rgyud): ci skad smras pa de de bzhin no// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang chos thams cad spros pa med pa ni byang chub ces bya'o// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur phyir pa 'khor de nyid du'ang
6a5(rgyud): rate 'dug pa des bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das kyis dkon mcho gtal la zhes bgyi ba'i ga
6a6(rgyud): bshad du gsol/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyang byang chub sems dpa' kun du 'azang po chos thams cad la thogs pa med pa'i spobs pa la gnas pa 'di la dris shig dang / 'dres
6a7(rgyud): khyod la sman par 'gyur ro// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon sa gyur dus bcom ldan 'das la mngan du phyogs te 'angag nas sor mo bcu thal mos te bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// ma
6a8(rgyud): khyer cing thams cad gzigs pa bcom ldan 'das nyid kyis ci'i slad du me bshad/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu gang na byang chub sems dpa' yod tan 'di lta bung
6b1(rgyud): padag 'khod pa den de bzhin gshegs pa rnams btang snyoms su bzhugs so// 'jam dpal gyis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams ni 'dir btang snyoms su bzhugs pa
6b2(rgyud): so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bung ni sems can gyi khams phal bar 'dor ba ma yin te/ rigs kyi bu 'on kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bstan pa ni bstan pa tshad med cing bstan pa
6b3(rgyud): bsam gyis mi khyab bo// de nas 'ang sa dpal gzhon nur gyur pas yang bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das kyis dkon mchog ta la la zhes bgyi ba'i gzungs bshad du ga se
6b4(rgyud): ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po 'di la dris shig dang / 'dis khyod la ston par 'gyur ro// 
6b5(rgyud): laganas pa'o// 'angs dpal gyis gsol pa/ gal te de bzhin gshegs pas bdag la dgong sun bdag gis skyes bu dam pa 'di la dri'ang bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal khyo
6b6(rgyud): dzen rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed thob pa yin na de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba gdab ci dgos/ rigs kyi khri khyod ni sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la skal 'dang ldan pa yin no// 'jam dpal gyis gsol
6b7(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das bdag gis sangs rgyas kyi chos gang dag kun du bsten pa dang / bskams pa dang mang du bgyis pa de thams cad ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i skyes bu'i mthung rig par bgyi'o// bcom ldan
6b8(rgyud): 'das kyis bka' phrul pa/ rigs kyi bu legs so legasas khyod kyis tshig 'di legs par smras te/ 'on kyang 'das dpal khyad la gsol ba 'debs kyis khyod byang chub sem 'daba' kun du la
7a1(rgyud): la dris shig/ de nas bcom ldan 'dang la 'jam dpal gnon nur gyur pas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po 'di ni shin tu za
7a2(rgyud): ste/ theg pa chen po rtogs par khong du chud pa lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal la/ rigs kyi bu spyod kyang chos thams cad kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal ba yin gyis bdag lam gsungs
7a3(rgyud): khyab pa dang ldan pa'o// de nas pa ma dpal gzhon nur gyur pas byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po la sor mo bcu'i
7a4(rgyud): sar te phyag 'tshal nas byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po la 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal ba'i sras khyod kyis bdag la skabs phyen khyad la bdag yi ge 'phruganyis shig 'dri'o// byang chub
7a5(rgyud): dpa'i kun du 'azang pom smras pa/ rigs kyi bu de'i dus la dbab par shes pan dris sheg/ de nas 'jam dpal gzhan nur gyur pas byang chu'ajams dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun du bzang po la 'di skad
7a6(rgyud): pas/ sems pa'is pa 'dus rgyas sangs rgyas shes bya ba gni ro dgang mim byang chung sems dpa' kun du babang pos smras bya/  rgyal ba'i sras sas rgyas kyi gni don nigazhi med pa'i don / 
7a7(rgyud): kyi gan 'jom ni dngos po med pa'i don to// sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i dan ni bsam gyis kyi khyab pa'i don to// sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i don no mo mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i don to// sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i ngo
7a8(rgyud): dngar ma// sangs rgyas rgyagano da ri zlas pa'angan do/ sangs rgyas bye gzhi'i donan blang ba mad pa 'dzin to// sangs rgyas kyi gzi'i don ni dong ba med pa'i don to/ sangs rgyas kye gzhi'i don nam
7b1(rgyud): ba' dang mtshungs pa'i don to// sangs rgyas kyi gzhi'i dod ni bskad du med pa'i don to// rigs kyi bu sangab rgyas kyi chos rnams kyi rang bzhin ni de lta bu yin no// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras ga
7b2(rgyud): sa thams cad spros pa med pa yin te/ 'o na sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams shes ji skad bstan/ byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bstan pa 'di ni bstan du med pa'o// 'jam dpal gyis
7b3(rgyud): kye rgyal ba'i sras bstan du med na ci zhig bstan/ byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos smras pa/ 'jam dpal bstan du med pa ni btags te bstan to// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras btags pa
7b4(rgyud): dka 'dogs par byed/ byang chub sems dpa' kun du bdang pos smras pa/ 'jam dpal btags pas ni dngos po yang mi 'dogs/ dngos po med pa yang ma 'dogs so// 'jam dpal gyis sbas pa/ kye rgyal ba 'asras
7b5(rgyud): la te btags pas dngos po yang mi 'dogs dngos po med pa yang mi 'dogs na theg pa gsum po dag ji ltar bstan/ byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang po smras pa/ 'jam dpa' khyod chos kyi dbyings cha
7b6(rgyud): ba la chags pa mam byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'jam dpal de bzhin gshegs pas chos thams cad ni dngos pa med pa'o zhes bstan pa'i phyir te/ gang dngos po med pa'i phyir zhe na/ phung po lnga dmigs pa
7b7(rgyud): 'i phyir ro// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ byang chub smos pa dang bcas pa yin nam/ 'on te spros pa med pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang pos smras pa/ rigs kyi bu byang chub ni spros pa dang bcas pa yang
7b8(rgyud): sapa med pa yang ma yin te/ 'di ltar byang chub dang / spros pa dang bcas pa dang / spros pa med pa ni gnyis su med de gnyis su dbyer med do// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' sems dang
8a1(rgyud): po dub pang dpol rigs kyi thang bca pa 'di legs so lags sa nas pa babyin no// gnas 'di brjod pas lnga dang bcas cing 'jig tan 'di chongs pa
8a2(rgyud): gyur ro// 'ang sa dpal gyis gsolapa/ bcom ldan 'das chos btsun pa 'dis pa 'tshal ba mi phyu/ bcim na das kyis bka' yul ga gas kyi ba de bzhin te rba ga grung
8a3(rgyud): /  nas bcom ldan 'das la 'jab dpal gzhon gyur pas 'di ska rdzas gsol te/ bcom ldan 'das chos thams cad shegs pa lagasas ge bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' yul gi rig
8a4(rgyud): legs pa com ldan 'dus kyis bka' stsal pa/ regs kyi pan /  gang su zhi / na na bcos pa la bya ma med pa dzims 'dres ga
8a5(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' gan dbabang bas rnam par dag pa sa bsten pa 'di legs pa sas lags so/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' phul pa/ rigs kyi bu de ni te/ gad
8a6(rgyud): zhin no// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang 'den chos thams cad len 'thun pa yin no// don chos kyi chang chen po yod do// de nas shing sa la chen po lta bu'i bram ze mnyan pa nyid du gnas pas bcom ldanal
8a7(rgyud): chagasal to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub ni mnyam pa nyid bsam gyis me khyab pa lags te/ de la yig mi dmigs/ tshig 'bum dmigs so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ 
8b1(rgyud): khud de bzhin te/ chos kyi dbyings la tshig 'bru mo sna / don kyang ma snang ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das la'ajam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das stong pa nyid kyi rgyu 'thun pa
8b2(rgyud): / lags/ rnam pa gang lags/ rtags gang lags/ mtshan ma gang lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal stong pa nyid ni brjo dang med pa/ bskrad du med pa ste brjod du med pa'i chos nyid
8b3(rgyud): nyid ces bya'o// stong pa nyid de ni yi ge me pa ste/ de'i phyir stong pa nyid ces bya'o// stong pa nyid do ni bskad du med pa ste/ de'i phyir stong pa nyid ces bya'o// rigs kyi bu chos thams cad ni
8b4(rgyud): nyid kyi stong ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa shA dang te'i bus 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i chos la gnas pa rnams kyi rnam
8b5(rgyud): 'phrul pa la gzigs/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal ge tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i shes pa ni mchog yin gyi dgra bcom pa'i shes pa ni de lta ma yin
8b6(rgyud): phying nam dgra bcom pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chog rnams las dang du gnas la/ byang chub sems dpa' de ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das su 'byung ba'i phyid do// de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' sa
8b7(rgyud): dzin po chos thams cad byed dbang byug gi rgyal pos 'di snyed ces gsol to// com ldan 'das de la bcom ldan dres kyis gsungs pa'i dzin bdag gis 'tshal ba ltar na nyan thos kyi chos rnams sa
8b8(rgyud): ba nyid lags sa/  com ldan dis kyis bka' stsal pa rigs kyi bu nan thas kyis nyan thob kyi chos rnams mthob ba ni yin to/ 'on kyang nyin thos la byang chub sems dpa' da ba stan cig kyis
9a1(rgyud): ba la lan gdab pa 'am/ spyod pa byin gyis brlab par bya ba'i nus pa dang mjug la yod/ de nas bcom ldan 'das pa la ma pal gzhon nur gyur pas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcortsa ldan
9a2(rgyud): shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pas shes rab dang ldan pa rnams kyi mchog tu bstan pa lags na bstan par 'di gang la bstan pa lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ 'ang mang ba le nga
9a3(rgyud): bstan pa 'di ni bstan pa med pa'o// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas gnas brtan shA ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad ces smras so// gnas brtan gyis nyan thos kyi chos rnams thob pam/ smras pa de
9a4(rgyud): yir no// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ 'o na ci khyod so so'i skye bo 'am/ smras pa de ni ma yin no// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ 'o na ci khyod slob pa 'am/ smras pa/ de ni ma yin no// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ 
9a5(rgyud): khyod ci shes rab dang ldan pa'i mchog yin nam/ smras pa de ni ma yin no// 'jam dpal gyis smras pa/ gal te btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu so so'i skye
9a6(rgyud): mchog kyang ma yin na de nyid khyod dmigs pa can du 'gyur ro// shA ra dwa ti'i bus smras pa/ rigs kyi bu kho bo ni skyes bu dam pa rgya mtsho ltar gting dpag dka' ba khyod dang 'gyed par mi byed do// 'jam dpa
9a7(rgyud): kyis smras pa/ btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu khyod ni rgan rabs thu bo mchog yin gyis btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu de skad ma zer cig/ gnas brtan gyis smras pa/ rags kyi'u rgas pa'i dngos pos ni ci yang 'thob par
9a8(rgyud): rararo// rims kyi 'u don de nyid zhes par bya ba'i rgyur khyod lang ba bya'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lnga ste dper na rdo rje dran don gyis kyang ri brag chen po rnam par 'jig go// sa
9b1(rgyud): bzhin du khyod kyi spu'i khung bu gcig na shes rab 'dug pa gang yin pa de na kho bo lta bu'i sems can rdul phra rab kyi rdub snyed rnams la med do// riyas kyi bu do nang nyid shes par bya ba'i phyir yang khyod la dpe bya'o// 
9b2(rgyud): bu 'di la skyed yin/ ba lang glang po tsho shin tu mi bzad pa chen pod yang mi stobs dang ldan pas lcags kyu chung ngus dul bar byed do// rigs kyi bu de bzhin du khyod ni stobs dang ldan pa// zo can nyam chung bste/ kla
9b3(rgyud): / chen po 'di lta bu dang kho bo 'gyed ga la nus/ de nas bcom ldan 'das la gnas brtan shA ra dwa ti'i bus 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ dper na mi dmus long ges shul du mchi ba 'am/ 
9b4(rgyud): khyer mthong bar yang rngo mi thog na/ khyim nas khyim du mchi ba'i ji lta ga la thog ste/ de ni gnas ma mchis so// de bzhin du glang po che chen po lta bu 'di dag gi mdun na bdag ri dmus long dang mtshungs par mthong
9b5(rgyud): sangs rgyas kyi chos 'di dag ni de tsam du rgya che ba lags so// bdag ni sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams kyi snod du ma gyur te/ da cab kyir yang ma mchis so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu des
9b6(rgyud): / zer cig/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu 'di lta ste/ dper na de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od kyis sems can ji snyed cig la reg pa de dag thams cad sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams thob pa yin no// shA ra dwa ti'i bu de bzhin du khyod na/ 
9b7(rgyud): 'dzin mtha' yas shing bsam gyis mi khyab pa thob pa yin no// bcom ldan 'das kyis chos kyi rnam grangs 'di bshad pa na/ lha dang mo'i skye dgu las sems can dku khre nyis stong gis chos mngon par rtog
9b8(rgyud): par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros byang chub semal dpa'i ni le la 'du dka nas
10a1(rgyud): blo gros snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu phyogs bcu'i phyogs re re'i 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed kyi pha rol nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan
10a2(rgyud): sangs rgyas kyi ning stong brag bcu'i rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed kyis// nal mngon par bstan / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag thams cad kyang mtshan rdo rje'i snying po zhes bya bar thu pan sug so
10a3(rgyud): / gcig ji lta bar phyogs bcu rnams nas kyang de bzhin te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dag gis de la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// chos kyi bro gros khyad de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin rgyu
10a4(rgyud): mtha' yas pa la snyoms par zhugs pa legs so legs so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad 'di nyid kyi
10a5(rgyud): dang / khyod nyid kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba nye bar bstan pas 'di las chos thams cad bsnyen par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rnam par spyang 'dig sangs rgyas kyil zhes rnam par 'phel bar dbya ba dang / chos
10a6(rgyud): dbyings su 'jug par bya ba dang / sems can gyi khams rnam pa dgrol ba dang / chags pa med pa'i ye shes la 'jug cing chud par bya ba dang// kun du sbyor bar bya ba dang / skad thams cad brjod par bya ba dang / thams cad
10a7(rgyud): mkhyen pa'i ye shes la 'jug par bya ba dang / chos thams cad la sleb pa med par bya ba dang / dus gsum thams cad yongs su shes pa'i chos bston pa la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir phyogs bcu nas de bzhin
10a8(rgyud): gshegs pa sangs rgyas kyi nang stong phrag bcu'i rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed thams cad kyang mtshan 'thun pa 'di dag thams cad khyod la byin gyis rlob kyis rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' nas
10b1(rgyud): gzhag pa bcu las brtsams te/ sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis chos bstan pa 'di la spobs pa skyed cig/ de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' bos// 
10b2(rgyud): gros la thogs pa med pa'i ye shes kyi snang ba dang / sleb pa med pa dang / chod pa med pa dang / brjed pa med pa'i chos nyid dang / tha dad pa med pa'i ye shes dang / kha nam tha pa med pa dang zil gyis mi nan pa dang / zhug
10b3(rgyud): pa dang / 'phogs pa med pa'i chos nyid dang / brjod pa bzang po nye bar sgrub pa mdzad de// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar ting nge 'dzin 'di nyid kyi chos nyid thob pa'i phyir ro// de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi
10b4(rgyud): phyag g.yas pa brkyang ste/ byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blagros kyi mgo la nyug pa mdzad de/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la reg ma theg tu de nas ting nge
10b5(rgyud): 'dzin de las langs nas byang chub sems dpa' de dkal smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rigs 'di ni 'di lta ste/ chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa dang / nam mkha'i khams kyi mthas pa
10b6(rgyud): pabs rgya che ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sas ngag 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams ni 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rigs su skye ba yin/ ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'a
10b7(rgyud): rnams kyi rigs su skye ba len/ da wa byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rigasas bye ba yin no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros la 'di skad ces
10b8(rgyud): smras so//  rgyal ba'i sras gang dag 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rags su skye ba'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pod dag na gang yin/ gangs
11a1(rgyud): khasams te krung sa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras drag byang chub sems dpar rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa bcu po de dag gang yin pa de shod cing de skad ces smras pa dang / byang
11a2(rgyud): sems dpa' chos kyi bla gros kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag sa ni bcu po 'dir
11a3(rgyud): / de dag ni 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis gsungs so// gsung // gsung bar 'gyur ro// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang
11a4(rgyud): mas dpa' rnam par gzhag pa dang / las dang po pa dang / rnal 'byor spyod pa dang / skye bar skyes pa dang / sbyor ba phun sum tshogs pa dang / bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa dang / phyir mi ldog pa dang / gnon nur gyu
11a5(rgyud): pa dang / rgyal tsha ba dang / dbang bsrung ba thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o// kye rgyal po'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa de bcu ci
11a6(rgyud): dag ste/ de dag ni 'das pa dang / mi byed pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis gsungs so// gsung ngo // gsung bar 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la sems dang po bskyed
11a7(rgyud): /  chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa gang zhe na/ kyo rgyal ba'i sras dag 'de la sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mthong ma thag tu gzugs bzang
11a8(rgyud): ma/ mdzes pa dag pa dog pa pangs rgyas pa'as/ rgya che ba laras the brjed che pa 'am rdzu 'phrul po rnam par 'phrul ba lagakun brjod pa'i rnam par 'phrul ba las/ rjes su bstan pa'i rnam 'ang phrul bya
11b1(rgyud): zed ngam/ sems can sdug bsngal ba dag mthong ngam/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsngags pa rgya cher thos na 'di lta ste/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes 'dod cing thog ma nyid du bla na med pa yang dag par
11b2(rgyud): rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed do// sems bskyed ma thag pa de nyid kyis bsnyen par dka' ba'i gnas bcu yongs su bzung bar 'gyur te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ gnas dang gnas pa yin pa shes pa dang
11b3(rgyud): 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar bang ba'i chos yang dag par blangs pa shes pa dang / thams cad du 'gro ba'i lam shes pa dang // khams du ma sna tshogs shes pa dang / mos pa dang rnam par grol ba dum rnas pa

11b5(rgyud): dang / sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa'i shes pa dang / lho'i mig gi shes pa dang / zag pazad pa shes pa ste/ bsnyen par dka' ba'i gnas bcu pa de dag yongs su bzung bar 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag
11b6(rgyud): sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de sangs rgyas mchod ba dag /

12a1(rgyud): nga sems bskyed ma zag pa de nyid kyis shes cher sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la sbyor zhing geng dug nas gang dag thos pa'i gnas de dag la yang bdag nyid ser kye/ gzhan gyi dring la
12a2(rgyud): mi 'jog pasob pa'i phyir // ke rgyal po sras dag 'di ni sems dang po bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dpar rnam par gzhag pa'o// kye rgyal ba 'i lus dag de la las dang po pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam byung
12a3(rgyud): kanag pa gapa nes/ kye rgyal pa'i sras dag 'di la las dang po pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni sems can rnams la thog ma nyid du sems rnam pa bcu bskyed de/ rnam pa bcugang ni/ 'di lta ste/ 
12a4(rgyud): sems dang bad bar bya ba'i sems dang / zh-ing brtse ba'i sems dang / mnyan pa sems dang / sdug pa'i sems dra phan gdags pa'i sems dang / kun du bsrung ba'i sems dang / snyoms pa'i sems dang / slob
12a5(rgyud): dpon kye sems dag stan pa'i sems te/ sems rnam pa bcu po 'di dag skyed do// kye rgyal ba'i sras dga' de ni las dang po ma'i byang chub sems dpa'o// kye rgyal ba 'i sras dag las dang po pa'i byang chub sems
12a6(rgyud): dpa' di lung banod pa dang // bton la skar bar bya'o// mang du pos nas rab tu dben pa la sbyang bar bya'o// rab tu dben pa byar nas dge 'a ba shes gnyen la mngon par dga' ba la sbyang bar bya'o// dge ba'i bshes gnyen
12a7(rgyud): de ba ga nas ngas shes pa la sbyar bar bya'o// sa shes par gyur nas mi byi gas pa la sbyar bar bya'o// ji 'jigs pa kur nam don / 
12a8(rgyud): pal sbyar bar bya'o// don shes par gyu nam chos kyi rjes su 'brang ba la sbyar bar bya'o// chos kyi rjes su 'brang ba sumanas brjed pa med pa'i chos nyid ma spyang bor bya'o// rmongs pa med par gyur nas chos nam
12b1(rgyud): bdag nyid skod kyi gzhan gyi dring la mo log pa thob pa'i phyir te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni las dang po pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de rnal 'byor skyong
12b2(rgyud): 'ibyang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa gang ne na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la rnal 'byor spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni dmigs pa rnam pa bcus chos rnams rtogs par byed de/ bcu gang de na/ 
12b3(rgyud): ltaste// chos thams cad la mi rtag pa nyid du rtogs par byed pa dang / chos thams cad la sdug bsngal ba nyid dang / bdag med pa nyid dang / stong pa nyid dang / g.yo ba med pa nyid dang / dbugs 'byin pa med pa nyid dang / 
12b4(rgyud): ding nyid dag rnam par rnyog pa mad pa cid dang rtsol ba med pa nyid dang mngon pa 'du byed pa med pa nyid rtogs par byed de tshul sangs su thung bar gyur ba'i byor myod bar mi byed ma skye mang mi byed
12b5(rgyud): rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni rnal 'byor spyod pa byang chub sems dpa'o// me rgyal ba'i sras dag rnal 'byor spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'adi ni sems can te khams brtag pa la spang bar bya'o// chos kyi dbyings
12b6(rgyud): brtag pa la sbyar bar bya'o// 'jig rten gyi khams brtag pa la skar ba / sa'i khams brtag pa la sbyar bar bya'o// chu'i khams dang me'i khams dang me drung gi khams dang nam mkha'i khams dang / gzugs kyi
12b7(rgyud): khams dang gzugs med pa'i khams btag pa la sbyar bar bya'o// de cir phyir zhen/ 'di ltar 'di ni shes cher chos rnams la sdang ba 'jug ci ga Na sa/ yo ga ded pa rang da nyid su chen/  mam
13a1(rgyud): 'jog pa thob pa'i phyir te/ kye rgyal po'i sras dag 'di ni rnal 'byor spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gzhag pa'o// kye rgyal 'a'i sras dag skye bar skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
13a2(rgyud): / rnam par gzhag 'a gang rjen/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di la skye bar skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni yongs su spyod par byed pa bcus gsung rab 'phags par skyes pa yin te/ bcu gang zhen 'di ltaste
13a3(rgyud): chos nyid las phyir mi zlog pa dang / sangs rgyas la mi phyed pa'i dad pa pathar thug par 'gyur ba yongs su lubya ba dang / chos nges par sems pa dang / sems cadan la rnam par dpyang pa dang zheng lu rnam pa
13a4(rgyud): pa dang / 'jig rten la rnam par dpyod pa dang / las la rnam par dpyod pa dang / rnam par smin pa pa rnam par dpyod pa dang / 'khor ba la rnam par dpyod pa dang / mya ngan las 'das pa la rnam par dpyod pa ste/ 
13a5(rgyud): yongs su spyong bar byed pa bcu'o dog gis gsung ngab 'phags par skyes pa med te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dge 'dage slo bar skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpa'o// kye rgyal ba'i bras dag skye bar skyes kyi
13a6(rgyud): chu sems dpa'adi ni das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos mnyam pa nyid rnam par dpyad pa la sbar bar bya'o// ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos mnyam pa nyid rnam par dpyad pa lasbyar bar ba'o// da ltar byung ba'i
13a7(rgyud): sangs rgyas kyi chos mnyam pa nyid rnam par dbyang ba la sbyar bar bya'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos mnyam pa nyid rnab par dpyad pa la sbar bar bya'i 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos yang dge bar 'a
13a8(rgyud): padam par dpya pal sbyar bar bya'o// mthon pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos yang dag par 'grub pa rnam par dpyad pa la rgyu rabar bya'o//  d+har byung ba re sangs rgyas kyi chos yang dag par 'grub pa rnamapa
13b1(rgyud): dpyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos gang dag par 'grub pa rnam par dpyad pa la sbyar bar bya'o// 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su 'grub pa mnya pa nyid rnam par dpyad pa la sna
